<div id="review_1760790690" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1760790690" />
    <a title="Jiana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana"><img alt="Jiana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540380229p2/10502567.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1760790690?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jiana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jiana" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana">Jiana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780142426272" href="/book/show/24611770-isla-and-the-happily-ever-after">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1760790690" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4809126889235431472"><blockquote>
  <i>“There's no story,' I say. 'I saw you one day, and I just knew.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I started Isla and the Happily Ever After with pretty low expectations. After reading Anna and the French Kiss and absolutely loving it, I picked up Lola and the Boy Next Door and absolutely hated it. This one turned out to be in between. I quite enjoyed it, but it wasn't as cute and good as Anna and the French Kiss.<br/><br/>I would describe Isla and Josh's relationship as cute and annoying at the same time. Some parts I was grinning lik</span>
  <span id="freeText4809126889235431472" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>“There's no story,' I say. 'I saw you one day, and I just knew.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />I started Isla and the Happily Ever After with pretty low expectations. After reading Anna and the French Kiss and absolutely loving it, I picked up Lola and the Boy Next Door and absolutely hated it. This one turned out to be in between. I quite enjoyed it, but it wasn't as cute and good as Anna and the French Kiss.<br /><br />I would describe Isla and Josh's relationship as cute and annoying at the same time. Some parts I was grinning like an idiot at how cute they were, other times I was rolling my eyes at how overly sappy they were. They're the type of couple who thinks it's the end of the world if they don't see each other a long time. Yeah, <b>no</b>. It's too sappy for my taste. <br /><br />Isla is... well, I really don't know how to describe her. She's adorable, but sometimes needy, immature and selfish. The way she handled issues related to Josh's ex, Rashmi, for example and how she treated her best friend, Kurt, at times, another example. As for Josh, <b>I love him</b>, okay. I love him a lot. I was excited to read his story ever since I finished Anna and the French Kiss. He's just so precious. He did mess up one big time in the book. I'm aware he didn't mean for it to seem that way, but <i>come on</i>, Josh sweetie, think.<br /><br />I absolutely loved the cameo at the end, basically all the characters from the previous books appear: Étienne, Anna, Lola, Cricket and Meredith. I smiled widely when Étienne showed up because I absolutely adore him. And Étienne and Anna are just aksjdsjkjksau, I love their relationship! Lola... well if you've read my Lola and the Boy Next Door review, you'd know I pretty much can't stand her and I never really cared for her and Cricket's relationship. Still, I loved the cameo as a whole!<br /><br />Weirdly, I enjoyed Stephanie Perkins's writing in Anna and the French Kiss. However, here? I didn't really like it. I was annoyed with it most of the time. <br /><br />I recommend this book because it serves its purpose. You want something fluffy, fast and cute? Definitely pick this one up, unless you haven't read Anna and the French Kiss before! Then definitely pick up Anna and the French Kiss first!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4809126889235431472" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Liam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34270521-liam"><img alt="Liam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415266097p2/34270521.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Liam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Liam" href="/user/show/34270521-liam">Liam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781409581130" href="/book/show/21850308-isla-and-the-happily-ever-after">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34270521-liam?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1086414646" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12100531804346695404">During the first half of the book I was slightly disappointed because everything was just too cliche and they fell in love so fast, I expected more from Stephanie Perkins... But then, she did it like she always does! THIS WOMAN IS A QUEEN!!! She manages to have control over my emotions with her perfect characters and writing, this book was no exception!<br/><br/>Isla and Josh were beyond cute and I fell in love with them from the very start (even from Anna and the French kiss!!). As I said, their relation</span>
  <span id="freeText12100531804346695404" style="display:none">During the first half of the book I was slightly disappointed because everything was just too cliche and they fell in love so fast, I expected more from Stephanie Perkins... But then, she did it like she always does! THIS WOMAN IS A QUEEN!!! She manages to have control over my emotions with her perfect characters and writing, this book was no exception!<br /><br />Isla and Josh were beyond cute and I fell in love with them from the very start (even from Anna and the French kiss!!). As I said, their relationship was slightly unrealistic to me but it all backfired later on, making it more believable. Their relationship captivated me I couldn't out this book down!<br /><br />It was nice to have a variety of scenery with this book! I loved going back to Paris but it was nice to have a bit of New York and Barcelona in there too! <br /><br />There is one part of this book when all the charcters from the series meet up and (I'm not going to spoil anything but if you've read it you'll know which bit I mean) I literally has goosebumps and was crying!!! These characters and their ADORABLE relationships are part of me and I really do love them to pieces! The ending was perfect too which just made everything even better!! <br /><br />I will love this series forever and I would absolutely love to see it made into films!! <br /><br />What an emotional roller coaster this series has took me on! I really do think these books have to be some of my favourites and I recommend them to all! Yes, they can be cringey and cliche but wHAT IS NOT TO LIKE ABOUT THAT??? Especially when it is done so well!!<br /><br />I will forever be thankful for the one and only Stephanie Perkins for this series, any book she writes in the future I will not think twice about buying! <br /><br />*hugs these books tightly for eternity*</span>
  <a data-text-id="12100531804346695404" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1243722123?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kai" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kai" href="/user/show/41788524-kai">Kai</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41788524-kai?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41788524-kai?shelf=to-buy">to-buy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41788524-kai?shelf=finished-series">finished-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1243722123" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2023943925626005525"><i>“Do adults realize how lucky they are? Or do they forget that these small moments are actually small miracles? I don’t want to ever forget.”</i><br/><br/>3.5/5 stars<br/><br/>Isla was not as good as Anna but way better than Lola. I enjoyed returning to Paris, but some of the magic in Anna was lost.<br/>Out of all the guys I liked Josh the most. It was interesting to read about how the relationship between the protagonists unfolds - in comparison to them usually having the first kiss on those last 50 pages. I really liked th</span>
  <span id="freeText2023943925626005525" style="display:none"><i>“Do adults realize how lucky they are? Or do they forget that these small moments are actually small miracles? I don’t want to ever forget.”</i><br /><br />3.5/5 stars<br /><br />Isla was not as good as Anna but way better than Lola. I enjoyed returning to Paris, but some of the magic in Anna was lost.<br />Out of all the guys I liked Josh the most. It was interesting to read about how the relationship between the protagonists unfolds - in comparison to them usually having the first kiss on those last 50 pages. I really liked that. Sexuality also plays a big part in this third installment, and it just seemed right. I did not have the feeling that it was rushed or awkward, no, it seemed fitting and it really surprised me, since sex is usually not a thing that happens too often in regular YA romance novels.<br />Of course, the melodrama could not be missing and it totally annoyed me again, destroying what was a wonderful relationship.<br />The ending was EXTREMELY cheesy. So cheesy. Cheesy.<br /><br /> <a href="https://www.instagram.com/fantasticbooksandwheretofindem" rel="nofollow noopener">Find more of my books on Instagram</a></span>

<div id="review_1224942458" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1224942458" />
    <a title="spencer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29377707-spencer"><img alt="spencer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605244321p2/29377707.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1224942458?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="spencer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="spencer" href="/user/show/29377707-spencer">spencer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1224942458" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16165738096301249019"><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“I am hard on myself. But isn’t it better to be honest about these things before someone else can use them against you? Before someone else can break your heart? Isn’t it better to break it yourself?” </i>
</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408777046i/10895968._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>___________________________________<br/><br/><br/>If you've read the first two books and haven't read this one yet, READ IT! If you have read it, please, someone, anyone, fangirl/fanboy with me because I need to talk about something that happened in this book! If you've read it, you'll know what I'm talking a</span>
  <span id="freeText16165738096301249019" style="display:none"><br><br><b>
  <i>“I am hard on myself. But isn’t it better to be honest about these things before someone else can use them against you? Before someone else can break your heart? Isn’t it better to break it yourself?” </i>
</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408777046i/10895968._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>___________________________________<br><br><br>If you've read the first two books and haven't read this one yet, READ IT! If you have read it, please, someone, anyone, fangirl/fanboy with me because I need to talk about something that happened in this book! If you've read it, you'll know what I'm talking about!!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437871183ra/15639427.gif" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is by far my favorite one in the trilogy/companion novel series, because everything from the past two books wraps up so nicely. When I first read Anna and the French Kiss, I wasn't impressed but the books have gone so far in the span on three books. <br><br>On to the actual book review:<br><br><b>
  <u>1) The Plot</u>
</b><br><br>Anna takes place in France, Lola takes place in San Francisco, and Isla takes place in Manhattan/France! The settings in these books are phenomenal, because she describes all the areas so well and it's amazing. I <b>LOVE</b> how she described New York!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437871872ra/15639511.gif" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Isla is a student at the School of America in Paris (SOAP), and this book revolves around her love for Josh who we first met in Anna and the French Kiss. Whenever this book first started off, it had me laughing out loud from page 2, because Isla had just gotten her wisdom teeth removed and she was loopy and hitting on Josh and AH. It was so good!<br><br>These books are so cute, and if you want to get out of a reading slump, these are the books for you.<br><br><b>
  <u>2) The Characters</u>
</b><br><br><b>Isla</b> - <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437872496i/15639727.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I cast Isla as Holland Roden from the MTV show Teen Wolf! I think Isla is my favorite narrator throughout these books! I just found myself relating to her so much, far more than I could relate to Anna or Lola, and I fell in love with her. <br><br><b>Josh</b> -<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437873340i/15639832._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I cast Josh as Robert Sheehan from the failure that was The Mortal Instruments movie. I love seeing Josh again, especially getting to go deeper in his character and see how sweet he was and how heartfelt, it was so nice to read from him again.<br><br><b>
  <u>3) The Writing</u>
</b><br><br><i> - “For a certain type of person, high school will always be brutal,' the head says. 'The best advice that I can give you is to figure out what comes next, and work towards that.” </i><br><br><i> - “... But we stayed together because... I don't know why. Maybe because we thought we should be in love. At least I did. I wanted to be in love.”</i><br><br><i> - “I'm... a blank canvas. There's nothing here to love.” </i><br><br><i> - “Phones are distracting. The internet is distracting.The way he looked at you? He wasn't distracted. He was consumed.” </i><br><br><i> - “Do adults realize how lucky they are? Or do they forget that these small moments are actually small miracles? I don’t want to ever forget.</i><br><br><b>
  <u>Conclusion</u>
</b><br><br>Without a doubt, my favorite installment!<br><br><i>★★★★.5/5!</i><br><br> <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16165738096301249019" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+36phn9/Jzw0Y18bTrV1GHBxx50jO0a+/fRovVjKNr/BWMBUxCHuVJNI63q5QH/Hpi4gVe22yNmmii4MlYnEJQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('XClB2sacJK43kaupjJa0dVVgDdrbeDsJxD4x2nrfVABmDygIfcLtxpC6H8h7Y76qgz/qEhX1tW6fQHdrt5ymmg==')})
  }
//]]>
